<Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipP4mrHYZ0_VMqRE07iThm1VeBIbvGLZrnlb_6yy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMVgn8XXrO7kxGnidJy6cO0XncSwQ3frxAsQT_A=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pics><user_name>Alex B< /user_name>< text>
""""""" So we tried out the newest brunch place in the block and I have to say that it was pretty delicious! Having said that, here is an orderly review of what we felt being there:

Atmosphere: Really casual and friendly. Our hosts were very nice and welcoming. We were briefly informed about the place and their services, which I think was great considering that a lot of place do not take the trouble to introduce what they have to offer to their customers. This is a great place to hang out for a brunch date, brunch with friends or even family!

Price: It is a little pricey, but personally I think that the quality of food and service that they provide is worth the price!

FOOD: We didn't want to dive into the whole gastro experience at a new place just yet, so we decided to start out with very generic brunch items and ordered the pot roast hash and eggs, the steak and eggs, coffee and a drink. They served us complimentary muffins before bringing our entrees. The food was delicious. The steak was cooked just right, the eggs and the pot roast hash was wonderful. The portion was great. The presentation was great. Love the way they served their drinks. The food was not bland and lacking seasoning.

Overall we had a very great first experience there and we are definitely going back. My boyfriend was in love with the size and weight of their fork . He usually does not like bulky and heavy forks used in many places which are apparently very uncomfortable to eat with. But I guess Restore kitchen won him in terms of cutlery as well!""""""""''

We went here because we wanted some good breakfast, and they did not disappoint. My recommendation would be to get the meat candy (bacon). It was absolute perfection. I came here as I was looking for the restaurant that was here prior, Carolyn's Cafe.  I saw it was a new place and wanted to give it a try.  As soon as I stepped in, my experience started on the wrong foot.  The person working the front appeared to be busy looking on his laptop and despite the "please wait to be seated sign" he barely looked up from the screen to point to a nearby table stating "right here."  In my opinion, that's not how you greet customers.

The wait staff were friendly and attentive and the food came out within a decent time frame.  The food itself wasn't very memorable although it wasn't outright bad.  It is a bit overpriced and I guess that extra money is going towards chilling tap water in glass bottles for the additional flair.  I probably wouldn't come here again due to my poor experience not meeting expectations for the price. Hopefully they have addressed these issues for other patrons.</Review>

< review>
This place has come to be like a second home to me. If you love beauty, fashion and entrepreneurship, this is the place for you! So many scrappy business people of all genders and nationalities trying to carve out their niche and live true American dream. Many of them already have but you wouldn’t know because they are forever humbled and focused on their next task.
Regardless of your place in the supply chain, you can find some business here to enhance your brand or personal use. Feel free to park on the street or in a garage and just walk around. Bring some sneakers and a cart with wheels as you may end up carrying more than you bargained for if not. The streets are endless. Weekends are for personal buyers and weekdays are generally for wholesale business buyers. Food options are limited unless you like Mexican food (then their endless). Your imagination and budget is the limit here!</review>

< Review>
I'm usually pretty handy with electrical work and do 95% of my own auto repair, so I decided I'd set the bar a notch higher - and bought a keyless entry system for my wife's car. I realized quickly that I was out of my element on this and need professional to handle this. But it was Sunday and everyone was closed.

Not at Advanced Car Stereo! They were not only open, but they took on my crazy project and finished it in just a couple hours. Poppers, wiring, installation (in a car with power nothing), etc. they did it all with a smile and everyone was really cool, friendly and helpful.

They have a TV they sling movies on all day, so you have something to do while you wait and the owners are really funny and knowledgeable. This is the third time throughout the years that I've come here and never have been dissatisfied. Their prices, for the quality of work, are very reasonable.

I highly recommend them.<//Review>

---- SHADY SHOP---

On Sunday, January 28, 2018 I stopped by Advanced Car Stereo because they were the closest. I needed to pick up (2) pairs of 6.5" speakers for my wife's car so I can replace the stock. They said they matched online prices, but still overcharge anyway. Basically online only means Crutchfield.

I had a $100 bill, and I said to add the $100 and charge the rest on my card. I made the mistake of assuming they would do it properly, I was distracted and in a hurry and wasn't really checking everything. Ronnie charged my card $150 and kept the $100. I didn't realize this until the following day when my wife asked why I spent $150 when she knew I had just gotten the $100 bill.

I drive down there with my receipt and told them what happened. I was nice at first, but they were like "we didn't see any $100 bill, you told us to put it all on the card" So then I just saw red, and I pointed at the kid who sold me the speakers and said "you know what you did, don't make me go down this road, it won't be good for any of you" I noticed they had cameras so I said check the footage. They told me that only the owner could, so I said call the owner then. They call him and he said he's busy, come back tomorrow at 9:30am and he will review the footage with me.

So I go there at 9:30, dude's not there. I asked the guy inside to call him and he said he doesn't have his number. I said of course you don't, you're just trying to cover for him now. I looked at the camera that was above where I was standing when I bought the speakers and noticed that the wire running to it was cut. Then I saw he had a sign that said he other stores, so I call the store in Temecula and ask to get the phone number for the owner. She won't give it out , and I told her it was regarding theft. She still wouldn't give it out but she would give a message. So I told her "tell Mo to give me back my money or the next phone call is to the police" and hung up.

Less than a minute later the phone rings and the guy answers it and is whispering in the corner. Then he starts counting money and gives me $100. He said "I'm just the middle man, I'm just doing what I'm told. Lovely customer service, told to lie and steal. Never again will I go here.</review>

<date>1547846159359</date><Rating>2< /Rating>< Text>
I wanted to love this place. The atmosphere was great and everyone was so nice. Great choice of tons of colors and a thorough pedicure.... but. I’m not one to complain, in fact I never have at any restaurant, salon... anything like that. But when I was getting my dip gel fill, I got cut twice pretty bad to where I was sore on those two fingers for days. Then, a week after... my polish started coming off 4 fingers. Now, about 8 days later, all the dip gel has lifted off four fingers and I have to pay for a whole new set. < text>
Recently bought a used car from this place. We made it clear it would be a cash purchase. When we got there, the first thing they did was pull our credit score without authorization. Young salesman said he didn't know why either, as we spoke multiple times about method of payment. We tried to make a quick and painless transaction by asking for $300 off (from a $13k vehicle), either off the price or $300 more for our trade in, which was already on the extreme low end. Sales manager would not budge, even brought in another manager to insult the value of our vehicle and proceed to moan about his cost and how much they're losing on the vehicle. At some point it got annoying enough we actually had to walked out. They made the young salesman walked out to our vehicle to stop us from leaving the parking lot and accepted our offer. <Text>Took my 2016 Honda Civic here in 2019 because the AC stopped blowing cold while it was still under warranty. This was the second time it had happened which I told them.  First time was handled by another Honda dealer when I lived in another area.

I was told it was checked for leaks and while the freon was very low, there were no leaks. They refilled the Freon and performed a scheduled maintenance check.

A little over one year later my AC stopped blowing cold air again. I took it back to Marin Honda at which time they then found a leaky valve.

It is obvious that the leak had been there since I purchased the car as the freon had to be recharged every year but the leak was not detected the first time I took it to Marin Honda while under warranty.

They didn't own up to the fact that they missed it the previous time I took it in with the same problem and said it was a maintenance issue. I asked if the valve only lasts 1-3 years and got no answer.

Overall the gentleman that was working with me was pleasant, professional, and did try to help but they refused to own up to their mistake and I had to pay for it. I can't trust their service department and I will not be back.

*Update - The manager said to send my info and he would contact me to try to remedy. I sent my info. He never reached out. The dishonesty is worse than if they had just let it go. Can't trust this dealership.

AC is not working again after a year. Same thing as every spring. They never fixed it. There was a class action lawsuit which says there is a problem with the condenser for these cars. I'll take it to a different Honda dealer to see if they will agree to fix it under the extended warranty on these AC condensers. This dealership is not honest.</Text>< pictures>

(Owner asked me on this post to email him so I did and he hasn't responded. Clearly not interested in resolving only public image.)

We did not buy a car here so I can't comment on the purchasing process. My frustration comes with feeling like we were misled over the phone. <Review>Today I experienced something to restore some of my (damaged) faith in human-kind:

My family bought a low-mileage certified Honda Insight from Marin five months ago. Marin received us late that day with tired children in tow, and stayed nearly two hours past regular closing time to complete our sale. The sales and financial people were sweet, courteous, and uncomplainingly worked overtime with us.

In those five months since, we put just over four-thousand miles on the car.
Last Sunday, I noticed that the front tires had prematurely and unevenly worn- to the point that they were nearly bald. Knowing this could be because of alignment or suspension, I called Marin. They asked me to bring it in the next day.

Here is where I fully expected to encounter baulking of some kind, and that I would have to argue the point of any misalignment as being responsible for the tire wear; in my head circulated tedious scenarios of letter-writing and explanation that I would have to undergo for some satisfaction, as the auto dealers I had encountered in the past fell under worse stereotypes of the profession.

Arriving at 9:30AM and explaining that I had to be back in the East Bay area to pick up my children from school, they prioritized my car. Still uneasy, I settled in the lounge with a free cappuccino and my book, thinking I would be there until the estimated 1:PM completion.
At 11:AM I was called to take my car.
They'd found and repaired the alignment issue and installed new tires at no charge to me. No argument, no hassle, pleasant, civilized, responsible, prompt- my God, what a relief! I'm so pleased- our experiences with Marin Honda have been some of the best we've had with any kind of business, ever.
Thanks, guys!< /Review><Pics>None< /Pics>< resp>
